 In the rainy season, clothes often smell bad
 kai baar to in kapadon par safed daag bhi ban jate hai
 This smell and stain may cause damping
 agar aapane kapade kisi aisi jagah rakhe hai jahaan sillen yaa nami bani rahati he to aapke kapade kharaab ho sakate hai
 This problem is more during the rainy season
 fafoond lagane kii vajah se kapadon se badboo aane lagati he
 In such a situation, if you want, you can save your clothes from getting moldy by adopting these measures
 1
 Thoroughly wipe with a dry cloth in the cupboard in which you want to keep clothes
 uske baad kapur ke pani se daraaj ko saaf karen
 Let it dry completely
 suukh jane ke baad hi kapade rakhen
 2
 keemtee or mahange kapadon ko plastic ke packet main yaa phir mote paper main lapetakar rakhen
 Apart from this, wax papers sold in the market are also very useful
 isse kapade sidhe almaari ke sampark main nahin aate hai or kharaab nahin hote
 3
 agar aapako lag rahaa he ki kuch kapadon main sillen aa gai he to sabase pehle in kapadon ko dhoop main acchhee tarah sukha len
 After that, wrap it in plastic bag and keep it inside
 4
 Open the cupboard once a week and leave it for a while
 isse hawa andar daraajon main ja sakegi
 Which will not cause damping
 5

 bangaloru ne dilashaan or captain viraat kohli (1) ke alaava abraham divilliars (7) ke wicket ganvaae

 ) r Varman (ratna Varman Shetty), the father of Abhishek Varman, director of Karan Johar's film Kalank, has passed away at the age of 72
 aisi khabaren hai ki unka nidhan cardiyak arest se hua
 Abhishek Varman cremated his father at the Oshiwara Crematorium
 spotboy ne mumbai mirar ke hawaale se likhaa- filmmekar karan johar, varun dhawan, arjuna kapur or aalia bhatta jaise sitare abhishek ko santvanaa dene pahunche
 r Varman was born in Mangalore
 aar varman mumbai jeje skool of art ke chaatr the
 After completing his studies, he started a publicity designing and cine advertising company
 dev anand production house unke major clients main se ek tha
 While working as a publicity designer, Varman became interested in art direction and worked as an assistant with famed art direction Sudhendu Roy for a few years before becoming an art director
 tab se ab tak varman ne 350 se zyada filmon main kaam kiya he
 It includes films like Betab, Khiladi, Khoon Bhari Mang, Karan Arjun, Andaz Apna Apna, Yeh Raat Hain Pyaar Ke, Boxer, Kaho Naa Pyaar Hai and Aitraj
 bataa den ki saal 1992 or 1993 main ham or angaar ke liye do baar sarvshereshth art diarection ke liye filmphere puraskaar bhi jeeta he

 co / stutfbaoru — Anupam Kher (@anupampkher) May 29, 2016 uttar pradesh main yogi sarkaar ke kisaanon ke ek lakh rupye tak ke karje maaf karne ke elaan ke baad ab punjab main bhi kisaanon ke karj maafee kii maang tej hone lagi he
 In fact, during the Punjab Assembly election campaign, Captain Amarinder Singh had promised the farmers of Punjab that they would forgive the entire loan amount of farmers when they came to power, and for this, Prashant Kishore's team and Congress workers asked the farmers of Punjab After filling a form, they were also given receipts
 ek campan chalaaya gaya tha jise naaraa diya gaya tha "karja kurki khatm or fasal kii puri rakam" yani kisaanon kaa karja maaf kiya jayega, unki jameen or sampatti kii kurki nahin hone di jaaegi or kisaanon se sarkaar jo fasal kharidegi uski puri rakam kaa bhugtan usee vakt kiya jayega
 Elections in Punjab were held with UP and the results of both the states were declared simultaneously
 isi vajah se ab akali dal congress sarkaar par dabaav bana rahaa he ki jaise upi kii yogi sarkaar ne apni pehali cabinet meeting main hi kisaanon ke karje maaf karne ko lekar faisla liya he vaise hi captain sarkaar bhi congress netritv kii ore se kisaanon ko kiye gayi karj maafee ke vaayade ko jald se jald puraa kare
 Former Punjab Chief Minister Parkash Singh Badal has also started pressuring the Captain government to fulfill this promise as soon as possible
